// Stop Post Quest
// ============================================================
moc_ruins,113,181,4	script	斯泰尔	4_M_ORIENT02,{
	mes "[斯泰尔]";
	mes "欢迎光临.欢迎您来到以制作^3355FF' 停止标志头饰 '^000000 闻名的斯泰尔家族商店.";
	next;
	mes "[斯泰尔]";
	mes "不知道您是否听过我们的家族史..";
	mes "我们家远早在以马车为主要交通工具时代就开始制作交通号志牌, 至今已经有两百五十年的历史了.";
	mes "近来我们常接到一些专门订购^3355FF' 停止标志头饰 '^000000 的订单, 现在流行将它拿来当装饰品.";
	next;
	switch( select( "订购^3355FF' 停止标志头饰 '^000000.:结束对话.")) {
	case 1:
		mes "由拥有两百五十年悠久历史的家族所制作的^3355FF' 停止标志头饰 '^000000发展出来的装饰品..";
		mes "有承袭着交通标志牌传统技术, 令人眼睛为之一亮且坚固耐用.";
		mes "相信一定不会使订购的顾客失望.";
		next;
		mes "订购^3355FF' 停止标志头饰'^000000 需要花费您^3355FF' 现金 91100 金币 '^000000 与 ..";
		mes "^3355FF' 木头 50 块 '^000000 还有 ^3355FF' 黑色染料 1 桶 '^000000 .";
		next;
		if ((countitem(1019) > 49) && (countitem(983) > 0) && (Zeny > 91099)) {
			delitem 1019,50;  //Wooden_Block
			delitem 983,1;  //Black_Dyestuffs
			Zeny -= 91100;
			mes "[斯泰尔]";
			mes "好了 !这是拥有两百五十年悠久历史的斯泰尔家族所制作的^3355FF' 停止标志头饰 '^000000 !";
			mes "谢谢您的光临, 欢迎下次再来!";
			getitem 2272,1; // Stop_Post
			close;
		}
		else {
			mes "[斯泰尔]";
			mes "您所准备的材料不足喔?";
			mes "请您再确认一下.";
			close;
		}
	case 2:
		mes "[斯泰尔]";
		mes "感谢您向斯泰尔家族订购商品.";
		mes "祝您事事顺心.";
		close;
	}
}

moc_ruins,118,176,4	script	炼金术公会	1_M_WIZARD,{
	mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
	mes "哈哈哈 - 又有顾客上门来啦!";
	mes "我知道你要说什么.";
	mes "你是为了魔法眼镜而来的对吧 ?";
	next;
	switch(select( "什么叫做魔法眼镜?:制作魔法眼镜.:跳过.")) {
	case 1:
		mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
		mes "是的 ! 它的正式名称应该是 ' ^3355FF望远镜^000000 ' !";
		mes "外型是长桶状, 里头";
		mes "有好几个玻璃片相叠在一起!";
		mes "它是利用光线反射的作用";
		mes "来看清楚在远方的东西";
		mes "近看的话是看不清楚的!";
		next;
		mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
		mes "觉得如何? 很棒吧?!";
		mes "阿哈哈哈哈!";
		mes ". . . . .";
		mes ".. 怎么 ?你看起来好像不太相信的样子?";
		mes "我说的可是真的?";
		next;
		mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
		mes "把制作望远镜所需要的东西";
		mes "一个一个记下来 ..";
		mes "^3355FF旋转镜片^000000 一个! ^3355FF钢铁^000000 一百片! 还有, 费用是 ^3355FF50000 金币^000000 !";
		close;
	case 2:
		if ((countitem(2243) > 0) && (countitem(999) > 99) && (Zeny > 49999)) {
			mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
			mes "好!希望这副眼镜能够给你带来更多的快乐";
			next;
			delitem 2243,1;  //Spinning_Eyes
			delitem 999,100;  //Steel
			Zeny -= 50000;
			mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
			mes "这就是了!魔法眼镜!";

			getitem 2296,1; // Binoculars
			next;
			mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
			mes "但是, 我必须先说明......";
			mes "不要用它来看你不该看的东西哦!哈哈哈哈??..";
			close;
		}
		else {
			mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
			mes "不够 ! 不够 ! 不够啊";
			mes "你怎么可以对在尘世大陆上最顶尖的炼金者";
			mes "那么不敬!";
			mes "真是太过分了";
		close;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[波立欧吉娜]";
		mes "喂喂喂喂!";
		mes "你这像是对";
		mes "在尘世大陆远近驰名";
		mes "的光学大师波立欧吉娜－我本人";
		mes "应该说的话吗 ? 说啊 ?!";
		close;
	}
}

que_job01,82,95,3	script	Bar Master#moc_main01	1_ETC_01,{
	if (checkweight(908,200) == 0) {
		mes "^3355FFWait a second!";
		mes "Right now, you're carrying";
		mes "too many things with you.";
		mes "Please come back after";
		mes "using the Kafra Service";
		mes "to store some of your items.^000000";
		close;
	}
	if (BaseClass == Job_Assassin) {
		mes "[Master]";
		mes "Please, come in.";
		mes "Care for a drink?";
	}
	else if ((BaseJob == Job_Thief) && (BaseClass != Job_Assassin)) {
		mes "[Master]";
		mes "......Huh. How did a ruffian like you get in here?";
		mes "Well, I guess Jack's not doing his job.";
		next;
		mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
		mes "Hey,master, don't be so harsh. We know each other, don't we?";
		mes "You don't wanna hurt your old friend's feeling~";
		next;
		mes "[Master]";
		mes "Whatever you say.";
		mes "So,what do you wanna drink?";
	}
	else {
		mes "[Master]";
		mes "....Hmm...";
		mes "What do you wanna drink?";
	}
	next;
	switch(select("Order a Drink:Ask About Mission:Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		mes "[Master]";
		mes "In this place, I only serve two drinks.";
		mes "You want a Tropical Sograt or";
		mes "a Vermilion on the Beach?";
		next;
		switch(select("Tropical Sograt:Vermilion on the Beach:Do you offer any free drinks?")) {
		case 1:
			if (checkweight(908,200) == 0) {
				mes "[Master]";
				mes "Hey, why did you bring";
				mes "so much stuff with you?";
				mes "I can't give you anything";
				mes "to drink if you don't have";
				mes "the room to carry it around.";
				mes "Clear out your inventory!";
				close;
			}
			else {
				if (BaseClass == Job_Assassin) {
					if (Zeny < 800) {
						mes "[Master]";
						mes "You know...";
						mes "I was going to charge you";
						mes "800 zeny for this drink, but";
						mes "it looks like you can't afford";
						mes "it right now. Come back when";
						mes "you have the zeny, alright?";
					}
					else {
						mes "[Master]";
						mes "Most bartenders would";
						mes "usually charge 1,000 zeny";
						mes "for this stuff, but I'll only";
						mes "ask you for 800. Enjoy it,";
						mes "my friend, and drink it as";
						mes "deeply as you would life.";
						Zeny -= 800;
						getitem 12112,1; //Tropical_Sograt
					}
					close;
				}
				else {
					if (Zeny < 1000) {
						mes "[Master]";
						mes "Hey, you don't have";
						mes "the zeny for this drink.";
						mes "Make sure you come back";
						mes "with 1,000 zeny if you want";
						mes "me to fix you something, okay?";
						close;
					}
					else {
						mes "[Master]";
						mes "For Assassins, I charge";
						mes "800 zeny, but for you, I'm";
						mes "gonna charge 1,000. No";
						mes "hard feelings, but you're";
						mes "already lucky to be here.";
						mes "Hey, enjoy your drink~";
						Zeny -= 1000;
						getitem 12112,1; //Tropical_Sograt
						close;
					}
				}
			}
		case 2:
			if (checkweight(908,200) == 0) {
				mes "[Master]";
				mes "Hey, why did you bring";
				mes "so much stuff with you?";
				mes "I can't give you anything";

				mes "the room to carry it around.";

			}

					if (Zeny < 800) {
						mes "[Master]";
						mes "You know...";
						mes "I was going to charge you";
						mes "800 zeny for this drink, but";
						mes "it looks like you can't afford";
						mes "it right now. Come back when";

					}

						mes "Most bartenders would";
						mes "usually charge 1,000 zeny";
						mes "for this stuff, but I'll only";

						mes "deeply as you would life.";

					}

				}
				else {

		else {
			if (BaseClass == Job_Assassin) {
				mes "[Master]";
				mes "Let me take a guess. You haven't been assigned any missions from this joint, eh?";
				mes "By the way, you like this place?";

				mes "got to focus on your training.";
				mes "And until you train... Why";
				mes "don't you enjoy a drink?";
				close;
			}
			else {
				mes "[Master]";
				mes "Mission...?";
				mes "Come on, what are";
				mes "you talking about?";
				mes "Stop talking crazy and";
				mes "order something to drink.";
				close;
			}
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Master]";
		mes "Hmmm.";
		close;
	}

	}

OnTouch:
	if (BaseLevel > 79) {
		mes "[大陆卫队 传令兵]";
		mes "请问你是... "+ strcharinfo(0) +"吗?";

		mes "[大陆卫队 传令兵]";
		mes "事态紧急, 请务必先听我说";
		close;
	}
	end;
}

moc_fild21,38,193,0	script	Morocc Timer#edq	-1,6,6,{
//OnInit:
//	set $@re_moc,0;
//	set $@re_moc_time$,"";
//	end;

OnTouch:
	if ($@re_moc == 0) {
		set $@re_moc,1;
		donpcevent "Satan Broadcast#edq::OnEnable";
	}
	end;
}

moc_fild21,1,1,0	script	Satan Broadcast#edq	CLEAR_NPC,{
OnInit:
	disablenpc "Satan Broadcast#edq";
	end;

OnEnable:
	enablenpc "Satan Broadcast#edq";
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer5000:
	mapannounce "moc_fild21","魔王梦罗克 : 连昆虫都不如的你们, 勇气真是可嘉啊...",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer15000:
	mapannounce "moc_fild21","魔王梦罗克 : 现在想后悔也来不及了, 甚至连后悔的时间也不会有的...",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer25000:
	mapannounce "moc_fild21","魔王梦罗克 : 再等一下吧... 可怜的家伙们, 再等一下下...",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

OnDisable:
	disablenpc "Satan Broadcast#edq";
	end;
}

		mes "望着无法形容的巨大黑暗时空的缝隙处, 被那压迫感惊吓而不自主的向后退了几步";
		next;
		mes "在充满光芒与黑暗浑沌的时空缝隙上, 感觉到强烈的阴森气息";
		next;
		mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
		mes "呜... 呜呜";
		close2;
		if($@re_moc == 1) {
			set $@re_moc,2;
			donpcevent "Satan Summon#edq::OnEnable";
		}
		end;
	}
	else {
		mes "望着无法形容的巨大黑暗时空的缝隙处, 被那压迫感惊吓而不自主的后退了几步";
		next;
		mes "在充满光芒与黑暗浑沌的时空缝隙上, 感觉到强烈的阴森气息";
		close;
	}

OnInit:
	enablenpc "黑暗之徒#edq";
	end;

OnEnable:
	enablenpc "黑暗之徒#edq";
	set $@re_moc_time$,"";
	end;

OnDisable:
	disablenpc "黑暗之徒#edq";
	donpcevent "时空的裂缝#edq::OnEnable";
	end;
}

moc_fild21,177,239,0	script	时空的裂缝#edq	CLEAR_NPC,1,1,{
	if ((rebirth_moc_edq == 4) && ($@re_moc == 3)) {
		mes "在魔王消失之后时空的缝隙处, 原本怵目惊心的黑暗气息也渐渐退散了";
		next;
		mes "在慢慢恢复平静的缝隙之处, 原本发出晶莹光芒的碎片也渐渐散去了";
		next;
		mes "伸手捡起了失去光芒的碎片";
		getitem 7820,1; //Morroc_Skin
		set rebirth_moc_edq,6;
		changequest 3053,3055;
		close;
	}
	else {
		mes "缓慢地...";
		mes "但非常紊乱又奇妙的黑暗之帷幕开始忙忙地散开";
		next;
		mes "感觉到若再靠近应该会有危险";
		close;
	}

OnInit:
	disablenpc "时空的裂缝#edq";
	end;

OnEnable:
	initnpctimer;
	enablenpc "时空的裂缝#edq";
	end;

OnDisable:
	stopnpctimer;
	disablenpc "时空的裂缝#edq";
	donpcevent "黑暗之徒#edq::OnEnable";
	set $@re_moc,0;
	end;

OnTimer1800000:
	set $@re_moc,4;
	end;

OnTimer21600000:
	stopnpctimer;
	set $@re_moc,0;
	donpcevent "时空的裂缝#edq::OnDisable";
	end;
}

moc_fild21,3,1,0	script	Satan Summon#edq	CLEAR_NPC,{
OnInit:
	disablenpc "Satan Summon#edq";
	end;

OnEnable:
	enablenpc "Satan Summon#edq";
	initnpctimer;
	monster "moc_fild21",177,217,"魔王梦罗克",1916,1,"Satan Summon#edq::OnMyMobDead";
	end;

OnDisable:
	stopnpctimer;
	killmonster "moc_fild21","Satan Summon#edq::OnMyMobDead";
	set $@re_moc,0;
	disablenpc "Satan Summon#edq";
	end;

OnMyMobDead:
	set $@re_moc,3;
	set $@re_moc_time$, gettimestr("%H%M%S",7);
	mapannounce "moc_fild21","我暂时让你们延残喘一下吧, 你们是找不到移往时空裂缝的我的!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	donpcevent "时空的裂缝#edq::OnEnable";
	donpcevent "Satan Broadcast#edq::OnDisable";
	donpcevent "黑暗之徒#edq::OnDisable";
	disablenpc "Satan Summon#edq";
	end;

OnTimer5400000:
	mapannounce "moc_fild21","要应付你们这些毛头小子还挺累人的!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	end;

OnTimer5415000:
	mapannounce "moc_fild21","我很忙, 我可没时间浪费在你们身上啦!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	stopnpctimer;
	killmonster "moc_fild21","Satan Summon#edq::OnMyMobDead";
	set $@re_moc,0;
	donpcevent "Satan Summon#edq::OnDisable";
	end;
}

			mes "Enable to enter to moc_fild21 field.";

			mes "^3131FF<Morroc>^000000";
			mes "Morroc has been summoned. After 90 minutes has passed, it will revert back to reset status.";
			mes "^3131FF<Continental Guards>^000000";
			mes "The warrior who has rebirth_moc_edq 4 ~ 7 is now enabled to enter to moc_fild21.";
		} else if ($@re_moc == 3) {
			mes "^3131FF<Morroc>^000000";
			mes "Morroc has been killed. Death time is "+$@re_moc_time$+"(00 hr/00 min/00 sec).";
			mes "After 6 hours later since the death time, it will be reset.";
			mes "The warriors whom has remained in the field can continue the quest via Time Space Gap.";
			mes "^3131FF<Continental Guards>^000000";
			mes "Disabled to enter to moc_fild21 from outside of the field.";
		} else {
			mes "^3131FF<Morroc>^000000";
			mes "Morroc has been killed. Death time is "+$@re_moc_time$+"(00 hr/00 min/00 sec).";
			mes "After 6 hours later since the death time, it will be reset.";
			mes "It has been already passed 30 minutes after Morroc's death, so warriors can not continue the quest even if they click the Time Space Gap.";
			mes "^3131FF<Continental Guards>^000000";
			mes "Disabled to enter to moc_fild21 from outside of the field.";
		}
		next;
		mes "[Helper]";
		mes "What do you want?";
		next;
		switch(select("Cancel.:Reset")) {
		case 1:
			mes "[Helper]";
			mes "Alright.";
			close;
		case 2:
			if (strnpcinfo(4) == "sec_in02")
				mes "You can reset at moc_fild21 5 5.";
			else {
				mes "Reset starts.";
				next;
				donpcevent "Group of Evil#edq::OnEnable";
				mes "Group of Evil NPC is appeared.";
				mes "Time-Space Gap NPC is disappeared.";
				mes "6 hours term timer is stopped.";
				donpcevent "Satan Summon#edq::OnDisable";
				mes "Morroc 90 minutes survival timer is stopped.";
				mes "Morroc is being killed.";
				mes "Now, Continental Guards will let players enter.";
			}
			close;
		}
	}
}

			next;
			mes "[班杰明]";

			mes "[班杰明]";
			mes "那也是一本畅销书.";
			next;
			mes "[班杰明]";
			mes "现在我要开始读这本书了,我会遇到我的玛莉,所以请不要打扰我.";
			next;
			mes "^660000在他看完以前,他逃避现实而在自己对玛莉的幻想中放纵.^000000";
			next;
			mes "^660000命运的痕迹,嗯?";
			mes "如果没有别的事情要做,我想去读这本书...^000000";
			next;
			mes "["+ strcharinfo(0) +"]";
			mes "等等,这是不是意味着我必须回到朱诺图书馆?";
			next;
			mes "^660000想起回到朱诺的艰辛你叹了一口气.^000000";
			changequest 2067,2068;
			close2;
			cutin "",255;
			end;
		}
		else if (barmunt_crow == 11) {
			mes "^660000你踏上了到朱诺的旅程,去阅读<命运的乌鸦>前传: <命运的痕迹>.^000000";
			close;
		}
		else if (barmunt_crow == 15) {
			if ((countitem(7797) == 1) && (countitem(7796) == 1)) {
				mes "["+ strcharinfo(0) +"]";
				mes "嗨, 班杰明!";
				mes "我有一件完美的东西可以让你引起玛莉的注意,想看看吗?";
				next;
				mes "[班杰明]";
				mes "什... 什么?!";
				mes "是什么东西? 让我看看!?";
				next;
				mes "^660000你拿出了一本有奥利弗席尔佩特亲笔签名的书.^000000";
				next;
				mes "[班杰明]";
				mes "我的天!";
				mes "这一定可以帮助我引起玛莉的注意!";
				mes "快把它给我!";
				next;
				switch(select("给他:不给他")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[班杰明]";
					mes " "+ strcharinfo(0) +"!";
					mes "你是最棒的!谢谢!";
					next;
					mes "[班杰明]";
					mes "玛莉~~!";
					mes "我明天清晨就去见她!玛莉,我来啦!";
					delitem 7797,1; //Author_Memo
					delitem 7796,1; //Author_Autograph
					set barmunt_crow,16;
					if (checkre(3))
						getexp 90000,90000;
					else
						getexp 900000,900000;
					close;
				case 2:
					mes "[班杰明]";
					mes "嗯?什么,你在逗我玩吗?";
					close;
				}
			}
			else {
				mes "[班杰明]";
				mes "阿...玛莉...阿...";
				close;
			}
		}
		else {
			mes "[班杰明]";
			mes "阿...玛莉...阿...";
			close;
		}
	}
	else {
		mes "这个男人看着手里的书,眼神里有着梦幻般的色彩.";
		close;
	}
}

prt_castle,391,205,3	script	王子#poe	4_M_6THPRIN1,{
	if (nk_prince > 6) {
		mes "[珀]";
		mes "无论发生什么,他就只是一个生活中的失败者.";
		close;
	}
	if (checkquest(10018) == 2) {
		mes "[珀]";
		mes "艾伦放弃了所有的竞争.即使有时候不得不得这样.他不如我,但是我对他很失望.";
		close;
	}
	else if (checkquest(10018) == 0 || checkquest(10018) == 1) {
		mes "[珀]";
		mes "......";
		close;
	}
	if (nk_prince < 5) {
		mes "[王子]";
		mes "你是谁?";
		mes "我觉得你不应该出现在这儿.";
		mes "还是你是为了鉴定继承人来的?";
		close;
	}
	else if (nk_prince > 4) {
		mes "[王子]";
		mes "过来这边.";
		mes "你是一位冒险家!";
		mes "我最爱挑战艰苦的冒险了.他们的冒险令我向往...你不能停止冒险...";
		next;
		mes "[王子]";
		mes "我的名字叫珀.";
		mes "我是理查德家族的王子.请你记住我,支持我...";
		next;
		mes "[珀]";
		mes "首先,我想测试你作为一个冒险家的能力.";
		mes "这不会很难,我只想知道你的直觉是否正确.";
		next;
		mes "[珀]";
		mes "我不想和一个直觉迟钝的人交谈.";
		mes "让我测试一下你的直觉.";
		next;
		mes "[珀]";
		mes "我有1到13号卡片,说出我选择的一张卡片的数字,是属于大的还是小的.";
		next;
		mes "[珀]";
		mes "对了,7是中间数.7代表不成功也不失败.这个游戏的目标是告诉我正确的数字,连续2次,让我们开始.";
		next;
		while(.@wincount < 2) {
			set .@card,rand(1,13);
			mes "[珀]";
			mes "好的,现在选择比较大或者较小的.";
			mes "只能选一种.";
			next;
			switch(select("大:小")) {
			case 1:
				mes "[珀]";
				mes "大吗?...";
				mes "我现在选择一张卡!";
				next;
				mes "[珀]";
				mes "我选择的是..." + .@card + "!!";
				next;
				if (.@card > 7) {
					set .@wincount,.@wincount+1;
					mes "[珀]";
					mes "哇,你答对了!";
					if (.@wincount == 2) {
						mes "你能连赢2次吗?...";
						next;
						break;
					}
					else {
						mes "但你还需要再答对了1次.";
						next;
					}
				}
				else if (.@card == 7) {
					mes "[珀]";
					mes "这次是中间数.";
					mes "下次再努力.";
					next;
				}
				else {
					mes "[珀]";
					mes "错误...";
					mes "希望下次你能有好运气.";
					close;
				}
				break;
			case 2:
				mes "[珀]";
				mes "小吗?...";

				}

			}
		}

	}
